  *    Rev 1.71   Apr 01 2013 11:04:06   AdilAwad
  * 1. Added data buffer overflow alarm.  This alarm will be raised if the ICS sends a "Get Data" command after the buffer overflows during a run.  This could happen if the Get data calls stop for an extended period of time because the TUV server is prempted or is suspended for an extended period of time.  
  * If the data buffer overflows and the next command that comes down from the ICS is "Get data" (presumably TUV server is no longer suspended or prempted) then the alarm is raised.  However, if a reset is received then the alarm is not raised as it means that the data system was restarted.

       public static string XmlToText(string xmlIn)
       {
           try
           {
               XmlDocument resultsDoc = new XmlDocument();
               resultsDoc.LoadXml(xmlIn);
               XmlNode resultsRoot = resultsDoc.DocumentElement;
               StringBuilder result = new StringBuilder();
               result.Append(Resources.GetString("TUVDetectorNoiseAndDrift_ResultsTitle"));
               result.AppendFormat(Resources.GetString("TUVDetectorNoiseAndDrift_ResultsDrift"),resultsRoot["Drift"].InnerText);
               result.AppendFormat(Resources.GetString("TUVDetectorNoiseAndDrift_ResultsNoise"),resultsRoot["SegPeakNoise"].InnerText);
 
               return result.ToString();
           }
           catch(Exception ex)
           {

     private void UpdateLampHistory()
       {
       lock (this)
         {
         string lampState;
         string currGoodIgnitions;
         string currTotalIgnitions;
         string[] historyStrings;
 
         XmlDocument tuvDoc = new XmlDocument();
         tuvDoc.LoadXml(iRemoteTUV.StatusXml);
         XmlNode tuvRoot = tuvDoc.DocumentElement;
 
         iRemoteTUV.GetLampHistory(out lampState, out currGoodIgnitions, out currTotalIgnitions, out historyStrings);
 
         this.goodIgnit.Text = currGoodIgnitions;
         this.totalIgnit.Text = currTotalIgnitions;
         this.currentState.Text = tuvRoot["Lamp"].InnerText;

         parameterForm.Minimum = 190.0F;
         parameterForm.Maximum = 700.0F;
 
         if (iRemoteTUV != null)
           {
           string statusXml = iRemoteTUV.TuvStatusXml;
           XmlDocument tuvDoc = new XmlDocument();
           tuvDoc.LoadXml(statusXml);
           XmlNode tuvRoot = tuvDoc.DocumentElement;
           XmlNode chARoot = tuvRoot["ChannelA"];
           parameterForm.SettingInvariant = chARoot["Wavelength"].InnerText;
           if (parameterForm.ShowDialog() == DialogResult.OK)
               TUVGlobals.Compat(iRemoteTUV.Name).SetWavelength(ServerLibEnum.TUVChannel.ChA, parameterForm.SettingValue);
           success = true;
           }
         }
       catch (Exception ex)
         {
         TraceLog.WriteException(ex);
         success = false;
         }
       return success;
       }

     /// SetLamp
     /// </summary>
     /// <returns></returns>
     public bool SetLamp()
       {
       bool success = false;
 
       try
         {
         if (iRemoteTUV != null)
           {
           string statusXml = iRemoteTUV.TuvStatusXml;
           XmlDocument tuvDoc = new XmlDocument();
           tuvDoc.LoadXml(statusXml);
           XmlNode tuvRoot = tuvDoc.DocumentElement;
 
           string lampState = tuvRoot["Lamp"].InnerText;
           bool isLampOn = (lampState == Resources.GetICSEnumeration("tLampState", "LampOn_3"));
 
           if (AcquityMessageBox.Show(
                string.Format(Resources.GetString("TUVControlPanel_SetLampCaption"), // "Turn lamp {0}?"
                  isLampOn ? Resources.GetString("TUVControlPanel_SetLampOn") /* "off" */ : Resources.GetString("TUVControlPanel_SetLampOff")),  // "on"
                Resources.GetString("TUVControlPanel_SetLampPrompt"),  // "Set Lamp"
                MessageBoxButtons.YesNo,
                AcquityMessageBox.MessageType.Ask,
-               (string)null,
-               "Preparing_the_System/Working_with_Instrument_Methods/turning_on_or_off_the_lamp.htm") == DialogResult.Yes)  //NOTRANSLATE
+               Identity.Info(), "HelpID_SetLamp") == DialogResult.Yes)  //NOTRANSLATE
             {
             iRemoteTUV.SetLamp(!isLampOn);
             }
 
           success = true;
           }
         }
       catch (Exception ex)
         {
         TraceLog.WriteException(ex);
         success = false;
         }
 
       return success;
       }

     private void MenuItemOnlineOffline(object sender, EventArgs e)
       {

   internal class ControlPanelContext : IDisposable
   {
       private static Mutex m = null;
       private bool isLocked = false;
 
       public ControlPanelContext()
       {
           Lock();
       }
 
       private void Lock()
       {
           if (m == null)
           {
               MutexCreator mc = new MutexCreator();
               m = mc.CreateMutexNoSecurity("TUVControlPanelContext");
           }
 
           isLocked = m.WaitOne();
       }

 namespace Waters.ACQUITY
 {
   [InitializeResources]
   internal class Resources : AcquityResources
   {
     private static System.Resources.ResourceManager rm = null;
     private static Assembly assy = null;
 
         private static IdentityInfo identityInfo = Identity.Info();
         private static string name = String.Empty;
 
         private static ResourceManager _Initialize(string nm, Assembly a)
         {
             SetCulture();
 
             ResourceManager rm = new System.Resources.ResourceManager(nm, a);
             return rm;
         }
 
     public static void Initialize(Assembly a)
       {
       if (rm == null)
         {
         assy = a;
 
-        //AssemblyName assyName = new AssemblyName(a.FullName);
-        //name = assyName.Name;
-        name = "Waters.ACQUITY." + identityInfo.ConsoleAssy;
+        string rescoll = identityInfo.GetIdentityString("ResourceCollection");
+        if (!string.IsNullOrEmpty(rescoll))
+            name = rescoll;
+        else
+            name = "Waters.ACQUITY." + identityInfo.ConsoleAssy;
 #if TUV140_COMPATIBLE
         name = name.Replace("140", "");
 #endif
 
         rm = _Initialize(name, assy);
 
         //AddICSResources( tuvType, icsToken, icsResourceFileName );
         if ((identityInfo != null) && identityInfo.IsValid)
           AddICSResources(identityInfo.InstrumentType, identityInfo.FilenameRoot, identityInfo.CoreResources, identityInfo.Resources);
         }
       }
 
     public static string GetString( string resourceName )
     {
       return GetString( resourceName, name, assy, ref rm );
     }
 
     public static string GetICSEnumeration(string typeName, string id)
       {
       //return GetICSEnumeration( icsToken, typeName, id );
       if ((identityInfo != null) && identityInfo.IsValid)
         return GetICSEnumeration(identityInfo.FilenameRoot, typeName, id);
       else
         return string.Empty;
       }

     private void wavelengthA_Click(object sender, System.EventArgs e)
       {
       if (isLampOn)
         {
         string currentWavelength = "";
         int i = wavelengthA.Text.IndexOf(' ');
         if (i > 0)
           currentWavelength = wavelengthA.Text.Substring(0, i);
 
-        //ParameterForm waveForm = new ParameterForm("acqtuv.chm::", "Preparing_the_TUV_Detector/setting_wavelengths.htm");
-        ParameterForm waveForm = new ParameterForm(helpFile, helpKeyword);
+        ParameterForm waveForm = new ParameterForm(Identity.Info(), "HelpID_SetWavelength");
         waveForm.Text = iRemoteTUV.ProductName;
         waveForm.Instrument = Resources.GetString("TUV_Name"); //"TUV";
         waveForm.Prompt = Resources.GetString("SetWavelengthA_Prompt"); // "Wavelength A:";
         waveForm.Units = Resources.GetString("Wavelength_Units"); // "nm";
         waveForm.DecimalPlaces = 0;
         waveForm.Setting = currentWavelength;
         waveForm.SetRange(190F, 700F);
         if (waveForm.ShowDialog() == DialogResult.OK)
           TUVGlobals.Compat(iRemoteTUV.Name).SetWavelength(ServerLibEnum.TUVChannel.ChA, waveForm.SettingValue);
         }
       }

 // FUNCTION

 /// <summary>OnSetActive
 /// </summary>
 //
 BOOL CAnalogOutPage::OnSetActive()
   {
   // If first time, load the data from the document
   if ( !m_dataLoaded )
     LoadDataFromDoc();
 
   m_helpCtrl.SetIcon( ((CMethodEditDlg*)GetParentDlg())->hHelpIcon );
 
   CoreTUVMethod* pMethod = GetParentDlg()->GetTUVMethod();
 
   if( pMethod )
     {
     CoreTUVChannel* pChannel = ( m_index == 0 ? &pMethod->channelA : &pMethod->channelB );
 
     int modeChoiceListToUse;
     if (pMethod->wavelengthMode == 1) //Single Wavelength mode
       modeChoiceListToUse = (m_index == 0) ? 0 : 2; //A-list or C-list
     else //Dual Wavelength mode
       modeChoiceListToUse = (m_index == 0) ? 1 : 2; //B-list or C-list
 
     pChannel->dataMode.SetActiveChoiceList(modeChoiceListToUse );
 
     CString strMode( (LPCTSTR)pChannel->dataMode );
     m_dataMode = strMode;
 
     UpdateData( FALSE );
 
     int iMode = (int)pChannel->dataMode;
 
     if( iMode == 6 ) //Ratio
       {
       m_ratioScalingMaxCtrl.EnableWindow( TRUE );
       m_ratioScalingMinCtrl.EnableWindow( TRUE );
       }
     else
       {
       m_ratioScalingMaxCtrl.EnableWindow( FALSE );
       m_ratioScalingMinCtrl.EnableWindow( FALSE );
       }
     }
 
-  CEditorPropertyPage::sFilename = Identity::GetIdentity()->m_helpFile;
-  CEditorPropertyPage::sHelpKeyword = Identity::GetIdentity()->m_helpKeywords.Get( IDD )->keyword;
+  context_Identity = Identity::GetIdentity();
+  context_HelpID = "HelpID_MethodTabAnalog";
 
   return CEditorPropertyPage::OnSetActive();
   }

 /// <summary>AcquireInstrumentStatus
 /// <para>
 /// Get the status and insterpret it in this instrument's context.
 /// </para>
 /// </summary>
 //
 bool CCoreTUVInstrComms::AcquireInstrumentStatus()
 {
     bool ret = false;
 
     try
     {
         //CoreTUVInstrStatusDetail *pStatus = static_cast<CoreTUVInstrStatusDetail *>(CurrentStatus());
 
       CInstrumentStatusLock status(this);
       STATUSCLASS* pStatus = static_cast<STATUSCLASS*>(status.CurrentStatus());
-
+    if( pStatus != NULL )
+    {
         //Uint8 lastStatus = pStatus->CoreTUVStatus.dataMode;
 
         ret = CInstrument::AcquireInstrumentStatus();
 
     if( HasFakeAlarm() )
       ++pStatus->CoreTUVStatus.ComStatus.alarmCount;
 
         if (ret )
         {
             //if( pStatus->HaveErrors() )
             //  SetConnectionState( CConnection::Error );
 
             CString theMode = StrState( pStatus->CoreTUVStatus.dataMode );
 
             switch ( pStatus->CoreTUVStatus.dataMode )
             {
             case ctrl_UNINITIALIZED:
             case ctrl_INITIALIZING:
             case ctrl_CALIBRATING:
                 SetConnectionState( CConnection::Unavailable );
                 break;
 
             case ctrl_SINGLE_WAVELENGTH:
             case ctrl_DUAL_WAVELENGTH:
         //When instrument finishes initializing transition to Idle state.
         if( GetConnectionState() == CConnection::Unavailable )
           SetConnectionState( CConnection::Idle );
                 break;
 
             case ctrl_SCAN_ACQUIRE_MODE:
             case ctrl_SCAN_PLAYBACK_MODE:
             case ctrl_IDLE_DATA:
             case ctrl_ERROR_MODE:
                 break;
 
             default:
                 SetConnectionState( CConnection::Disconnected );
                 break;
             }
             DiagnosticLog( DiagLevelD, _T("Status"), _T("Current mode is %s"), theMode );
         }
+    }
     }
     catch(...)
     {
     }
 
     return ret;
 }

 // FUNCTION

 /// <summary>GetAlarm
 /// </summary>
 //
 bool CCoreTUVInstrComms::GetAlarm()
 {
     bool ret = false;
 
   bool fakeAlarm = HasFakeAlarm();
     ret = CDetectorInstrument::GetAlarm();
 
     if( ret )
     {
         //CoreTUVInstrStatusDetail *pStatus = static_cast<CoreTUVInstrStatusDetail *>(CurrentStatus());
 
     CInstrumentStatusLock status(this);
     STATUSCLASS* pStatus = static_cast<STATUSCLASS*>(status.CurrentStatus());
 
+  if( pStatus != NULL )
+  {
         WatersXmlEnum* pNextAlarm = &pStatus->m_xml.ledAlarm.type;
         CCoreTUVInstrAlarmData* pAlarm = static_cast<CCoreTUVInstrAlarmData*>(CurrentAlarm());
 
         // Assign alarm ID into WatersXmlEnum to look up localized text
     bool temp = WatersXmlVariable::OptimizeAssignments;
     WatersXmlVariable::OptimizeAssignments = false;
         *pNextAlarm = pAlarm->Type();
     WatersXmlVariable::OptimizeAssignments = temp;
 
         CString rawText = pAlarm->NativeText();
         CString nativeString = rawText;
 
         CString localizedString = (BSTR)(*pNextAlarm);
         if( (int)(*pNextAlarm) < 0 )         // no localized matching string found?
             localizedString = rawText;
 
         // Firmware version 1.10 does not support formattable messages. For now, if we find a parenthesized suffix
         // appended to the returned text, we will copy it to the returned message (even though it may contain
         // English text)
 
         int len = rawText.GetLength();
         if( rawText[len-1] == TCHAR(')') )
         {
             int index = rawText.Find( TCHAR('(') );
             if( index > 0 )
             {
                 CString suffix = rawText.Mid( index );
 
                 localizedString.Append( _T(" ") );
                 localizedString.Append( suffix );
 
                 nativeString.Append( _T(" ") );
                 nativeString.Append( suffix );
             }
         }
 
         pAlarm->SetText( localizedString, nativeString );
 
     if( fakeAlarm && pAlarm->Type() > 0 )
       SetAlarm( pAlarm->Type(), pAlarm->Text(), pAlarm->NativeText() );
+  }
     }
     return ret;
 }

+  {
+    WatersXmlDocument* pDoc = &pStatus->m_xml;
+    CInstrument::SetAlarm( pDoc, alarmType, alarmText, nativeText );
+  }
 }

 /// <summary>__Identify
 /// </summary>
 //
 void CoreTUVInstrObject::__Identify(BSTR configurationName, int desiredOptions, bool bCreateThread, struct IInstrument* pInstr)
   {
   m_configurationName = CString(configurationName);
   Instrument()->CurrentStatus()->SetName( m_configKey );
 
   CString mutexName;
   mutexName.Format( "IDENTIFYLOCK_%s", m_configurationName );
   CMutex mutex( FALSE, mutexName, s_CSecurityAttrib.GetFullAccessAttributes() );
   CSingleLock lock( &mutex );
   if( !lock.Lock( 60000 ) )
     {
     PerformanceLog( "TIMEOUT", "Error in CoreTUVInstrObject::__Identify(), %s", m_configurationName );
     return;
     }
 
   m_configKey = m_configurationName;
 
   //RunTimeInMethod should persist if it is ever set.
   m_opts = desiredOptions | (m_opts & InstrClient_RunTimeInMethod);
 
+  LaunchConsole(FALSE);
   GetClientBuffer();
